extern int bar();

int
main()
{

        if (foo()) {
            rc = 1;
        } else {
            rc = 1;
        }
    } else {
        if (foo()) {
            rc = 1;
        } else {
            rc = 1;
        }
    }
    int a = 1;

    return rc;
}
